    @pytest.mark.timeout(900, func_only=True)
    def test_logical_PBM_T307(start_cluster, cluster):
        """
        Test Case PBM-1681: Selective snapshot restore will not restore changes recorded by oplog capture on config shard
    
        Test checks that when documents are added during the oplog slicing phase, they are included in the backup.
        Steps:
            1: Add 100k documents to the test.data collection and 1k into the test.data2 collection.
            2: Logical backup occurs
            3: Searching for log 'dump collection "test.data2" done'. When it is found 2 more documents are added.
            4: A restore is performed with the new backup.
            5: A check is performed to verify that the two new added documents are present in the restored collection as well as the original 10k.
        """
        cluster.check_pbm_status()
        client = pymongo.MongoClient(cluster.connection)
    
        client["test"]["data"].insert_many([{"x": (i + 1), "pad": "x" * 2000} for i in range(100000)])
        client["test"]["data2"].insert_many([{"x": (i + 1), "pad": "x" * 2000} for i in range(1000)])
    
        backup_result = {"backup_full": None}
    
        def run_backup():
            backup_result["backup_full"] = cluster.make_backup("logical")
    
        backup_thread = threading.Thread(target=run_backup)
        backup_thread.start()
    
        target_log_pattern = 'dump collection "test.data2" done'
        max_wait_time = 300
        start_time = time.time()
        log_found = False
        log = re.compile(r'\[rscfg/rscfg01:27017\][^\n]*dump collection "test\.data2" done')

                client["test"]["data2"].insert_many(documents_post_snapshot)
                log_found = True
    
            if time.time() - start_time > max_wait_time:
                Cluster.log("Timeout waiting for log pattern")
                break
    
        backup_thread.join()
        assert log_found, f"Targeted log {target_log_pattern} not found"
        backup_name = backup_result["backup_full"]
    
        pre_restore_count = client["test"]["data2"].count_documents({})

        result = cluster.exec_pbm_cli(f"describe-backup {backup_name} --out=json")

        cluster.make_restore(backup_name, restore_opts=["--ns=test.data2"], restart_cluster=False, check_pbm_status=True)

    @pytest.mark.timeout(900, func_only=True)
    def test_logical_PBM_T307(start_cluster, cluster):
        """
        Test Case PBM-1681: Selective snapshot restore will not restore changes recorded by oplog capture on config shard
    
        Test checks that when documents are added during the oplog slicing phase, they are included in the backup.
        Steps:
            1: Add 100k documents to the test.data collection and 1k into the test.data2 collection.
            2: Logical backup occurs
            3: Searching for log 'dump collection "test.data2" done'. When it is found 2 more documents are added.
            4: A restore is performed with the new backup.
            5: A check is performed to verify that the two new added documents are present in the restored collection as well as the original 10k.
        """
        cluster.check_pbm_status()
        client = pymongo.MongoClient(cluster.connection)
    
        client["test"]["data"].insert_many([{"x": (i + 1), "pad": "x" * 2000} for i in range(100000)])
        client["test"]["data2"].insert_many([{"x": (i + 1), "pad": "x" * 2000} for i in range(1000)])
    
        backup_result = {"backup_full": None}
    
        def run_backup():
            backup_result["backup_full"] = cluster.make_backup("logical")
    
        backup_thread = threading.Thread(target=run_backup)
        backup_thread.start()
    
        target_log_pattern = 'dump collection "test.data2" done'
        max_wait_time = 300
        start_time = time.time()
        log_found = False
        log = re.compile(r'\[rscfg/rscfg01:27017\][^\n]*dump collection "test\.data2" done')
    
        while backup_thread.is_alive() and not log_found:
            result = cluster.exec_pbm_cli("logs --tail=10000")
            out = result.stdout
    
            if log.search(out):
                print("DOCUMENTS ADDED")
                client["test"]["data2"].insert_many(documents_post_snapshot)
                log_found = True
    
            if time.time() - start_time > max_wait_time:
                Cluster.log("Timeout waiting for log pattern")
                break
    
        backup_thread.join()
        assert log_found, f"Targeted log {target_log_pattern} not found"
        backup_name = backup_result["backup_full"]
    
        pre_restore_count = client["test"]["data2"].count_documents({})
        Cluster.log(f"Pre-restore document count in test.data2: {pre_restore_count} (expected 1002)")
    
        result = cluster.exec_pbm_cli(f"describe-backup {backup_name} --out=json")
        Cluster.log(f"Backup description: {result.stdout}")
    
        cluster.make_restore(backup_name, restore_opts=["--ns=test.data2"], restart_cluster=False, check_pbm_status=True)

start_cluster = True, cluster = <cluster.Cluster object at 0x7fbdf2417b90>

    @pytest.mark.timeout(900, func_only=True)
    def test_logical_PBM_T307(start_cluster, cluster):
        """
        Test Case PBM-1681: Selective snapshot restore will not restore changes recorded by oplog capture on config shard
    
        Test checks that when documents are added during the oplog slicing phase, they are included in the backup.
        Steps:
            1: Add 100k documents to the test.data collection and 1k into the test.data2 collection.
            2: Logical backup occurs
            3: Searching for log 'dump collection "test.data2" done'. When it is found 2 more documents are added.
            4: A restore is performed with the new backup.
            5: A check is performed to verify that the two new added documents are present in the restored collection as well as the original 10k.
        """
        cluster.check_pbm_status()
        client = pymongo.MongoClient(cluster.connection)
    
        client["test"]["data"].insert_many([{"x": (i + 1), "pad": "x" * 2000} for i in range(100000)])
        client["test"]["data2"].insert_many([{"x": (i + 1), "pad": "x" * 2000} for i in range(1000)])
    
        backup_result = {"backup_full": None}
    
        def run_backup():
            backup_result["backup_full"] = cluster.make_backup("logical")
    
        backup_thread = threading.Thread(target=run_backup)
        backup_thread.start()
    
        target_log_pattern = 'dump collection "test.data2" done'
        max_wait_time = 300
        start_time = time.time()
        log_found = False
        log = re.compile(r'\[rscfg/rscfg01:27017\][^\n]*dump collection "test\.data2" done')
    
        while backup_thread.is_alive() and not log_found:
            result = cluster.exec_pbm_cli("logs --tail=10000")
            out = result.stdout
    
            if log.search(out):
                print("DOCUMENTS ADDED")
                client["test"]["data2"].insert_many(documents_post_snapshot)
                log_found = True
    
            if time.time() - start_time > max_wait_time:
                Cluster.log("Timeout waiting for log pattern")
                break
    
        backup_thread.join()
        assert log_found, f"Targeted log {target_log_pattern} not found"
        backup_name = backup_result["backup_full"]
    
        pre_restore_count = client["test"]["data2"].count_documents({})
        Cluster.log(f"Pre-restore document count in test.data2: {pre_restore_count} (expected 1002)")
    
        result = cluster.exec_pbm_cli(f"describe-backup {backup_name} --out=json")
        Cluster.log(f"Backup description: {result.stdout}")
    
        cluster.make_restore(backup_name, restore_opts=["--ns=test.data2"], restart_cluster=False, check_pbm_status=True)
    
        document_count = client["test"]["data2"].count_documents({})

    @pytest.mark.timeout(900, func_only=True)
    def test_logical_PBM_T307(start_cluster, cluster):
        """
        Test Case PBM-1681: Selective snapshot restore will not restore changes recorded by oplog capture on config shard
    
        Test checks that when documents are added during the oplog slicing phase, they are included in the backup.
        Steps:
            1: Add 100k documents to the test.data collection and 1k into the test.data2 collection.
            2: Logical backup occurs
            3: Searching for log 'dump collection "test.data2" done'. When it is found 2 more documents are added.
            4: A restore is performed with the new backup.
            5: A check is performed to verify that the two new added documents are present in the restored collection as well as the original 10k.
        """
        cluster.check_pbm_status()
        client = pymongo.MongoClient(cluster.connection)
    
        client["test"]["data"].insert_many([{"x": (i + 1), "pad": "x" * 2000} for i in range(100000)])
        client["test"]["data2"].insert_many([{"x": (i + 1), "pad": "x" * 2000} for i in range(1000)])
    
        backup_result = {"backup_full": None}
    
        def run_backup():
            backup_result["backup_full"] = cluster.make_backup("logical")
    
        backup_thread = threading.Thread(target=run_backup)
        backup_thread.start()
    
        target_log_pattern = 'dump collection "test.data2" done'
        max_wait_time = 300
        start_time = time.time()
        log_found = False
        log = re.compile(r'\[rscfg/rscfg01:27017\][^\n]*dump collection "test\.data2" done')
    
        while backup_thread.is_alive() and not log_found:
            result = cluster.exec_pbm_cli("logs --tail=10000")
            out = result.stdout
    
            if log.search(out):
                print("DOCUMENTS ADDED")
                client["test"]["data2"].insert_many(documents_post_snapshot)
                log_found = True
    
            if time.time() - start_time > max_wait_time:
                Cluster.log("Timeout waiting for log pattern")
                break
    
        backup_thread.join()
        assert log_found, f"Targeted log {target_log_pattern} not found"
        backup_name = backup_result["backup_full"]
    
        pre_restore_count = client["test"]["data2"].count_documents({})
        Cluster.log(f"Pre-restore document count in test.data2: {pre_restore_count} (expected 1002)")
    
        result = cluster.exec_pbm_cli(f"describe-backup {backup_name} --out=json")
        Cluster.log(f"Backup description: {result.stdout}")
    
        cluster.make_restore(backup_name, restore_opts=["--ns=test.data2"], restart_cluster=False, check_pbm_status=True)

    @pytest.mark.timeout(900, func_only=True)
    def test_logical_PBM_T307(start_cluster, cluster):
        """
        Test Case PBM-1681: Selective snapshot restore will not restore changes recorded by oplog capture on config shard
    
        Test checks that when documents are added during the oplog slicing phase, they are included in the backup.
        Steps:
            1: Add 100k documents to the test.data collection and 1k into the test.data2 collection.
            2: Logical backup occurs
            3: Searching for log 'dump collection "test.data2" done'. When it is found 2 more documents are added.
            4: A restore is performed with the new backup.
            5: A check is performed to verify that the two new added documents are present in the restored collection as well as the original 10k.
        """
        cluster.check_pbm_status()
        client = pymongo.MongoClient(cluster.connection)
    
        client["test"]["data"].insert_many([{"x": (i + 1), "pad": "x" * 2000} for i in range(100000)])
        client["test"]["data2"].insert_many([{"x": (i + 1), "pad": "x" * 2000} for i in range(1000)])
    
        backup_result = {"backup_full": None}
    
        def run_backup():
            backup_result["backup_full"] = cluster.make_backup("logical")
    
        backup_thread = threading.Thread(target=run_backup)
        backup_thread.start()
    
        target_log_pattern = 'dump collection "test.data2" done'
        max_wait_time = 300
        start_time = time.time()
        log_found = False
        log = re.compile(r'\[rscfg/rscfg01:27017\][^\n]*dump collection "test\.data2" done')

            result = cluster.exec_pbm_cli("logs --tail=10000")

            if log.search(out):

                client["test"]["data2"].insert_many(documents_post_snapshot)
                log_found = True
    
            if time.time() - start_time > max_wait_time:
                Cluster.log("Timeout waiting for log pattern")
                break
    
        backup_thread.join()
        assert log_found, f"Targeted log {target_log_pattern} not found"
        backup_name = backup_result["backup_full"]
    
        pre_restore_count = client["test"]["data2"].count_documents({})
        Cluster.log(f"Pre-restore document count in test.data2: {pre_restore_count} (expected 1002)")
    
        result = cluster.exec_pbm_cli(f"describe-backup {backup_name} --out=json")
        Cluster.log(f"Backup description: {result.stdout}")
    
        cluster.make_restore(backup_name, restore_opts=["--ns=test.data2"], restart_cluster=False, check_pbm_status=True)

    @pytest.mark.timeout(900, func_only=True)
    def test_logical_PBM_T307(start_cluster, cluster):
        """
        Test Case PBM-1681: Selective snapshot restore will not restore changes recorded by oplog capture on config shard
    
        Test checks that when documents are added during the oplog slicing phase, they are included in the backup.
        Steps:
            1: Add 100k documents to the test.data collection and 1k into the test.data2 collection.
            2: Logical backup occurs
            3: Searching for log 'dump collection "test.data2" done'. When it is found 2 more documents are added.
            4: A restore is performed with the new backup.
            5: A check is performed to verify that the two new added documents are present in the restored collection as well as the original 10k.
        """
        cluster.check_pbm_status()
        client = pymongo.MongoClient(cluster.connection)
    
        client["test"]["data"].insert_many([{"x": (i + 1), "pad": "x" * 2000} for i in range(100000)])
        client["test"]["data2"].insert_many([{"x": (i + 1), "pad": "x" * 2000} for i in range(1000)])
    
        backup_result = {"backup_full": None}
    
        def run_backup():
            backup_result["backup_full"] = cluster.make_backup("logical")
    
        backup_thread = threading.Thread(target=run_backup)
        backup_thread.start()
    
        target_log_pattern = 'dump collection "test.data2" done'
        max_wait_time = 300
        start_time = time.time()
        log_found = False
        log = re.compile(r'\[rscfg/rscfg01:27017\][^\n]*dump collection "test\.data2" done')

                client["test"]["data2"].insert_many(documents_post_snapshot)
                log_found = True
    
            if time.time() - start_time > max_wait_time:
                Cluster.log("Timeout waiting for log pattern")
                break
    
        backup_thread.join()
        assert log_found, f"Targeted log {target_log_pattern} not found"

        result = cluster.exec_pbm_cli(f"describe-backup {backup_name} --out=json")

    @pytest.mark.timeout(900, func_only=True)
    def test_logical_PBM_T307(start_cluster, cluster):
        """
        Test Case PBM-1681: Selective snapshot restore will not restore changes recorded by oplog capture on config shard
    
        Test checks that when documents are added during the oplog slicing phase, they are included in the backup.
        Steps:
            1: Add 100k documents to the test.data collection and 1k into the test.data2 collection.
            2: Logical backup occurs
            3: Searching for log 'dump collection "test.data2" done'. When it is found 2 more documents are added.
            4: A restore is performed with the new backup.
            5: A check is performed to verify that the two new added documents are present in the restored collection as well as the original 10k.
        """
        cluster.check_pbm_status()
        client = pymongo.MongoClient(cluster.connection)
    
        client["test"]["data"].insert_many([{"x": (i + 1), "pad": "x" * 2000} for i in range(100000)])
        client["test"]["data2"].insert_many([{"x": (i + 1), "pad": "x" * 2000} for i in range(1000)])
    
        backup_result = {"backup_full": None}
    
        def run_backup():
            backup_result["backup_full"] = cluster.make_backup("logical")
    
        backup_thread = threading.Thread(target=run_backup)
        backup_thread.start()
    
        target_log_pattern = 'dump collection "test.data2" done'
        max_wait_time = 300
        start_time = time.time()
        log_found = False
        log = re.compile(r'\[rscfg/rscfg01:27017\][^\n]*dump collection "test\.data2" done')

            out = result.stdout

                client["test"]["data2"].insert_many(documents_post_snapshot)
                log_found = True
    
            if time.time() - start_time > max_wait_time:
                Cluster.log("Timeout waiting for log pattern")
                break
    
        backup_thread.join()
        assert log_found, f"Targeted log {target_log_pattern} not found"
        backup_name = backup_result["backup_full"]
    
        pre_restore_count = client["test"]["data2"].count_documents({})
        Cluster.log(f"Pre-restore document count in test.data2: {pre_restore_count} (expected 1002)")
    
        result = cluster.exec_pbm_cli(f"describe-backup {backup_name} --out=json")
        Cluster.log(f"Backup description: {result.stdout}")
    
        cluster.make_restore(backup_name, restore_opts=["--ns=test.data2"], restart_cluster=False, check_pbm_status=True)

    @pytest.mark.timeout(900, func_only=True)
    def test_logical_PBM_T307(start_cluster, cluster):
        """
        Test Case PBM-1681: Selective snapshot restore will not restore changes recorded by oplog capture on config shard
    
        Test checks that when documents are added during the oplog slicing phase, they are included in the backup.
        Steps:
            1: Add 100k documents to the test.data collection and 1k into the test.data2 collection.
            2: Logical backup occurs
            3: Searching for log 'dump collection "test.data2" done'. When it is found 2 more documents are added.
            4: A restore is performed with the new backup.
            5: A check is performed to verify that the two new added documents are present in the restored collection as well as the original 10k.
        """
        cluster.check_pbm_status()
        client = pymongo.MongoClient(cluster.connection)
    
        client["test"]["data"].insert_many([{"x": (i + 1), "pad": "x" * 2000} for i in range(100000)])
        client["test"]["data2"].insert_many([{"x": (i + 1), "pad": "x" * 2000} for i in range(1000)])
    
        backup_result = {"backup_full": None}
    
        def run_backup():
            backup_result["backup_full"] = cluster.make_backup("logical")
    
        backup_thread = threading.Thread(target=run_backup)
        backup_thread.start()
    
        target_log_pattern = 'dump collection "test.data2" done'
        max_wait_time = 300
        start_time = time.time()
        log_found = False
        log = re.compile(r'\[rscfg/rscfg01:27017\][^\n]*dump collection "test\.data2" done')

                client["test"]["data2"].insert_many(documents_post_snapshot)
                log_found = True
    
            if time.time() - start_time > max_wait_time:
                Cluster.log("Timeout waiting for log pattern")
                break
    
        backup_thread.join()
        assert log_found, f"Targeted log {target_log_pattern} not found"

        pre_restore_count = client["test"]["data2"].count_documents({})

        result = cluster.exec_pbm_cli(f"describe-backup {backup_name} --out=json")
        Cluster.log(f"Backup description: {result.stdout}")
    
        cluster.make_restore(backup_name, restore_opts=["--ns=test.data2"], restart_cluster=False, check_pbm_status=True)
